


### Basic Physics Lab - Uses vanilla icon
   building_physics_lab_0 = { 
      base_buildtime = 210
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = no }
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 60
      }
   
      required_resources = {
         energy = 1.5
      }
      produced_resources = {
         physics_research = 3
      }
      upgrades = { building_physics_lab_1 }
      prerequisites = { "tech_scientific_method" }
   
      potential = {
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
            any_tile = {
                has_resource = {
                  type = physics_research
                  amount > 0
               }
            }
         }
      }
   
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_physics_research"
            tile = {
               has_resource = {
                  type = physics_research
                  amount > 0
                     }
               }
            }
      }
      ai_allow = {
         is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 10
      }
   }
   
### Physics Lab II - Uses vanilla icon
   building_physics_lab_1 = { 
      base_buildtime = 180
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = no }
      is_listed = no
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 120
      }
   
      required_resources = {
         energy = 2
      }
      produced_resources = {
         physics_research = 5
      }
      upgrades = { building_physics_lab_2 }
      prerequisites = { "tech_physics_advanced_19" }
   
      potential = {
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
         }
      }
   
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_1"
            planet = { has_at_least_capital_1 = yes }
       }
      }
      ai_allow = {
         is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 1
      }
   }

### Supercollider - Uses vanilla icon
   building_physics_lab_4 = { 
      base_buildtime = 180
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = no }
      is_listed = no
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 320
      }
   
      required_resources = {
         energy = 3.5
      }
      produced_resources = {
         physics_research = 11
      }
      planet_modifier = {
         tile_resource_physics_research_mult = 0.05
      }
      prerequisites = { "tech_physics_unified_22" }
   
      potential = {
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
            is_capital = yes
         }
      }
   
      destroy_if = {
         planet = { is_capital = no }
      }
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_3"
            planet = { capital_building_3 = yes }
       }
      }
      ai_allow = {
         is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 1
      }
   }
   
### Holosuite Entertainment Center
   building_holodeck_1 = { 
      base_buildtime = 360
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = no }
      tags = { cultural_building }
      planet_unique = yes
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 300
      }
   
      required_resources = {
         energy = 5
      }
      planet_modifier = {
         pop_happiness = 0.05
      }
      upgrades = { building_holodeck_2 }
      prerequisites = { "tech_physics_computing_40" }
   
      potential = {
         owner = {
            is_borg_empire = no
         }
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
         }
      }
   
      produced_resource_trigger = {
         modifier = {
            has_valid_civic = civic_virtuoso
            resources = {
               unity = 1
            }
         }
         modifier = {
            has_valid_civic = civic_prophet_2
            resources = {
               unity = 0.5
            }
         }
      }
      destroy_if = {
         exists = owner
         owner = { is_borg_empire = yes }
      }
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_2"
            planet = { has_at_least_capital_2 = yes }
       }
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 10
      }
   }
   
### Omicron Holo Field Projector
   building_holodeck_2 = { 
      base_buildtime = 720
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = no }
      tags = { cultural_building }
      empire_unique = yes
      is_listed = no
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 500
         influence = 100
      }
   
      required_resources = {
         energy = 10
      }
      produced_resources = {
         physics_research = 5
      }
      planet_modifier = {
         pop_happiness = 0.10
      }
      prerequisites = { "tech_physics_omicron_28" }
   
      potential = {
         owner = {
            is_borg_empire = no
         }
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
         }
      }
   
      produced_resource_trigger = {
         modifier = {
            has_valid_civic = civic_virtuoso
            resources = {
               unity = 5
            }
         }
         modifier = {
            has_valid_civic = civic_prophet_2
            resources = {
               unity = 0.5
            }
         }
      }
      destroy_if = {
         exists = owner
         owner = { is_borg_empire = yes }
      }
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_2"
            planet = { has_at_least_capital_2 = yes }
       }
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 10
         modifier = {
            weight = 0
            from = { sector_controlled = yes }
         }
      }
   }

      base_buildtime = 180
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = no }
      tags = { power_plant }
      is_listed = no
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 150
      }
   
      produced_resources = {
         energy = 6
      }
      upgrades = { building_power_plant_5 }
      prerequisites = { "tech_physics_artificial_116" }
   
      potential = {
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
         }
      }
   
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_2"
            planet = { has_at_least_capital_2 = yes }
       }
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 1
         modifier = {
            weight = 0.25
            is_slave_tile_or_planet = yes
         }
      }
   }

### Pergium Power Plant - Icon might need work
   building_pergium_power_plant_0 = { 
      base_buildtime = 240
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = no }
      tags = { power_plant }
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 150
      }
   
      produced_resources = {
         energy = 10
      }
      prerequisites = { "tech_engineering_pergium_592" }
   
      potential = {
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
            any_tile = {
                has_resource = {
                  type = sr_pergium_5
                  amount > 0
               }
            }
         }
      }
   
      allow = {
         AND = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_sr_pergium_5"
            tile = {
               has_resource = {
                  type = sr_pergium_5
                  amount > 0
                     }
               }
            }
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_1"
            planet = { has_at_least_capital_1 = yes }
       }
         }
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 10
         modifier = {
            weight = 0.25
            is_slave_tile_or_planet = yes
         }
      }
   }
   
### Polaric Ion Power Station

      base_buildtime = 120

         minerals = 100

      }

      }
      prerequisites = { "tech_physics_field_manipulation_117" }
   
      potential = {
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
         }
      }
   
      allow = {
         AND = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requirement_not_homeworld"
            planet = {
               NOT = { has_modifier = "capital" }
               }
            }
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_1"
            planet = { has_at_least_capital_1 = yes }
       }
         }
      }
      ai_allow = {
         has_resource_block = no

         }
         modifier = {
            weight = 0.25
            is_slave_tile_or_planet = yes
         }
      }
   }

   building_school_0 = { 
      base_buildtime = 210
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = no }
      tags = { academic_building }
      planet_unique = yes
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 100
      }
   
      required_resources = {

      }

         engineering_research = 1
         society_research = 1
      }
      upgrades = { building_uniwing_2a building_uniwing_2b  building_uniwing_2c  }
      prerequisites = { "tech_society_interstellar_446" }
   
      potential = {
         owner = {
            is_borg_empire = no
         }
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
         }
      }
   
      produced_resource_trigger = {
         modifier = {
            has_policy_flag = policy_flag_edu_accelerated
            resources = {
               physics_research = 2
               engineering_research = 2
               society_research = 2
            }
         }
         modifier = {
            has_policy_flag = policy_flag_edu_private
            resources = {
               energy = 2
            }
         }
         modifier = {
            has_policy_flag = policy_flag_edu_social
            resources = {
               sr_prosperity_26 = 1
            }
         }
         modifier = {
            has_policy_flag = policy_flag_edu_religious
            resources = {
               unity = 2
            }
         }
         modifier = {         has_policy_flag = policy_flag_edu_propoganda
            resources = {
               influence = 0.05
            }
         }
      }
      destroy_if = {
         exists = owner
         owner = { is_borg_empire = yes }
      }
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_1"
            planet = { has_at_least_capital_1 = yes }
       }
      }
      ai_allow = {
         has_resource_block = no
         is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 1
      }
   }

### Slave Processing Facility - Uses vanilla icon
   building_slave_processing = { 
      base_buildtime = 360
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = no }
      planet_unique = yes
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 250
      }
   
      required_resources = {
         energy = 3
      }
      produced_resources = {
         food = 2
         minerals = 2
      }
      planet_modifier = {
         slave_mineral_output = 0.15
         slave_food_output = 0.15
         country_unrest_unhappy_slave_effect_mult = -0.33
      }
   
      potential = {
         owner = {
            is_borg_empire = no
            has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_domination_protection_racket
         }
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
         }
      }
   
      destroy_if = {
         exists = owner
         owner = { is_borg_empire = yes }
      }
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_1"
            planet = { has_at_least_capital_1 = yes }
       }
      }
      ai_allow = {
         has_resource_block = no
         planet = {
            count_pops = {
               limit = { is_enslaved = yes }
               count > 2
            }
         }
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 10
         modifier = {
            weight = 0
            from = { sector_controlled = yes }
         }
      }
   }

      }

         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = yes

                has_resource = {
                  type = physics_research
                  amount > 0
               }
            }
         }
      }

         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_physics_research"
            tile = {
               has_resource = {
                  type = physics_research
                  amount > 0
                     }
               }
            }
      }
   }

      base_buildtime = 180
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = yes }
      tags = { medical_building }
      icon = "Suliban_Light_Blue"
      planet_unique = yes
      is_listed = no
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 250
      }
   
      required_resources = {
         energy = 4
      }
      planet_modifier = {
         pop_growth_speed = 0.25
      }
      upgrades = { space_building_frontier_clinic_4 }
      prerequisites = { "tech_society_new_worlds_1104" }
   
      potential = {
         owner = {
            is_borg_empire = no
         }
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = yes
         }
      }
   
      produced_resource_trigger = {
         modifier = {
            has_policy_flag = policy_flag_health_private
            resources = {
               energy = 2
            }
         }
         modifier = {
            has_policy_flag = policy_flag_health_social
            resources = {
               sr_prosperity_26 = 1
            }
         }
         modifier = {
            has_policy_flag = policy_flag_health_university
            resources = {
               society_research = 5
            }
         }
         modifier = {
            has_policy_flag = policy_flag_health_growth
            resources = {
               food = 4
            }
         }
      }
      destroy_if = {
         exists = owner
         owner = { is_borg_empire = yes }
      }
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_2"
            planet = { has_at_least_capital_2 = yes }
       }
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 10
      }
   }

### Civilian District
   space_building_arcology_1 = { 
      base_buildtime = 360
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = yes }
      tags = { housing_construction }
      icon = "Suliban_Light_Blue"
      planet_unique = yes
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 200
      }
   
      required_resources = {
         energy = 2
      }
      produced_resources = {
         sr_prosperity_26 = 2
      }
      planet_modifier = {
         pop_happiness = 0.01
         pop_growth_speed = 0.05
      }
      upgrades = { space_building_arcology_2 }
      prerequisites = { "tech_engineering_materials_1439" }
   
      potential = {
         owner = {
            is_borg_empire = no
         }
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = yes
            any_tile = {
                has_resource = {
                  type = food
                  amount > 0
               }
            }
         }
      }
   
      produced_resource_trigger = {
         modifier = {
            has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_prosperity_trans_stellar_corporations
            resources = {
               unity = 1
               sr_prosperity_26 = 1
            }
         }
      }
      destroy_if = {
         exists = owner
         owner = { is_borg_empire = yes }
      }
      allow = {
         AND = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_food"
            tile = {
               has_resource = {
                  type = food
                  amount > 0
                     }
               }
            }
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_1"
            planet = { has_at_least_capital_1 = yes }
       }
         }
      }
   }
